I live in an unincorporated area of Placer County just west of the Roseville City limits.   I had two stray dogs come into my farm. <Pics>None<//Pics><response>{'time': 1578949135238, 'text': 'Hi Kim,\n\nWe are sorry for your frustration. The Placer SPCA provides all of our services to residents in Placer County with the exception of accepting strays from outside the city limits of Roseville.  We are legally unable to do so unless the city or county contracts with us for that service.  This helps to ensure that animals found in a particular jurisdiction are housed to be reunited with their owner in the appropriate facility.\n\nWe do accept owner surrendered animals from throughout Placer County and we visit other shelters frequently to bring animals into our adoption program once the legally mandated holding periods have expired.  Our spay neuter assistance program, SOS program funding veterinary, boarding and rental deposits, low cost rabies and vaccinations, food closet, humane education, kids clubs, kids camp, classroom programs, boys and girl scout programs,  and behavior assistance are available to all residents in Placer County. Really nice since the new building. Roomy, inviting clean.  Why are all the cats on gabapentin?!!!!???? I found that bizzarre!!!!

Update and change of opinion

This review is for Placer SPCA in general.I live on a Major Street and my daughter's cat who she got in the fall was with me while she was in LA so she got out and I had called Placer SPCA and said that it was having a difficult time getting her to come back in the house cuz. I had called them and asked for a trap and they told me that traps were only 4 capture ferrel  and spay and not for a cat who got out and you can't catch them.

I called animal control and they told me they didn't have any drops and to call the pound.  I had a large bowl on the front porch with water and I would feel it in the morning with water and ice cubes and I put a mix of dry food and canned food on the front porch and would feed Kitty.

I'm not sure if it's the folks that bought the house a few doors down from me because Kitty like to sleep on the previous tenants porch or if it was someone who was walking up and down the street that decided that Kitty was a stray and they took her and I'm not certain where they took her because when the poundgive my daughter the cat for some reason or another her information associate with the microchip was deemed as private. So if you took the cat to say the Atlantic Street but they couldn't call my daughter and say hey we have your cat they could only notify the microchip plays which would send you an email. to complicate matters my daughter had moved to LA and changed her phone number and forgot to change her number on kitties microchip.

I didn't tell you the cat was missing because I was seeing the cat on the daily and feeding it and putting water out for it and I knew that she was okay haven't seen her in a couple of days but something was eating the food and drinking the water.

lo and behold I get a text message from a kid saying why didn't you tell me kitties. I called the microchip place and they say the cat Placer SPCA.

now apparently this cat was captured once before before my daughter adopted it with no records attached to my daughter whatsoever.  And I called and I asked how much could kitty's bail was.

they transfer me to the old location I guess where they store recovered animals.  And I was told that she was there since the 28th and we're at like maybe the 16th because I was down in La visiting. and they said that being that she was a stray once before even though it wasn't under my name that she was a stray before and so it was $45 + $15 a day plus another charge because it's the second time she was brought in as a stray. Long story short kitties bail was $345. I was so heated with your information that they gave me that I just said keep the cat because number one she was not a stray she likes to go outside she likes to hang out on the front porch she likes to watch people go by she was well-fed she had food she had water someone was coming and feeding and watering while I was in Los Angeles. all this organization is to reunite pet owners with their pets why in the world would they make it cost prohibitive to for lack of a better word redeem your pet and go and pick it up when it was turned in.

First of all someone took it upon themselves turn in the, second of all no one fully explained my daughter the privacy settings on the microchip would prevent her from getting phone calls if something were to happen to, which delayed the process in collecting said said lost but not really lost pet. which just increase the cost to redeem the pet to an egregious amount we're even someone who is of comfortable means would balk at paying $345 to get their pet back.

that being said I will never advocate for the Placer SPCA ever to Infiniti again, nor will I donate one thin dime to them.

I'm still too annoyed to even think of calling them entering to negotiate be kitties fees.< /Review>

<review>Be aware they will not adopt rabbits to outdoor homes. This was not listed anywhere on their website (not even the downloadable forms, checklists, etc) and I wasted time and money going to learn this. Not to mention the disappointment. They literally would not adopt them to me.

I'm bummed that this location would rather let these animals sit in a small cage inside rather than adopt them to a loving home with lots of space outside.

Plenty of people keep rabbits outside and as a shelter I believe they shouldn't be so picky. These animals needs homes! I wonder how many other great homes have been denied the animals who stay here??!

In my specific example they have THREE rabbits that must be adopted TOGETHER, to an INDOOR home. This seems unlikely and the employee even said they had been there a while. I did a lot of research before deciding to adopt an outdoor rabbit and for every person who says indoor only there is another who says outdoor is fine.

Do they adopt cats and dogs to indoor homes only?

I really hope they reconsider this policy. It seems like a personal opinion, which is fine to have, but please let us choose....

Policies like this actually support backyard breeding, and helps continue the cycle of animals in shelters. Not only are they helping create more animals, they are simultaneously denying homes to these same animals. A double whammy to the pet population.

To give meaning to the previous paragraph I will give an example: now that I have been denied by the SPCA my only option is to get bunnies from a backyard breeder. This directly supports backyard breeding. As you know the leftover bunnies will end up at the SPCA waiting for an indoor home. They didn't get adopted the first time around, to indoor OR outdoor homes. What are the chances they will get adopted the second or third time around, when you cut the housing prospects in half? Not only this but the bunnies I get from a backyard breeder might be sexed wrong and result in 8 more bunnies in the shelter. Since my backyard breeder bunnies aren't fixed, and I don't want to pay for the procedure, these bunnies also end up at the SPCA. 8 babies, 2 parents, plus the 3 they refused me. This policy might result in 13 bunnies in the shelter, PER PERSON! Not to mention the parents brothers and sisters from the backyard breeder.

PLEASE CHANGE YOUR POLICY ON INDOOR ONLY HOMES!

The picture is my lovely outdoor rabbit hutch. It's a bit overgrown since nothing is eating the grass!<//review>< userid>

Fortunately we have tremendous programs that help us reunite lost animals with their owners and we have a hugely successful adoption program. < Text>
I really enjoyed this place.

The prices are based off of how many toppings or type of dough you use. The build your own pizza aspect of the restaurant is great and the prices are not bad for what you can get.

Toppings include standard choices like mozzarella cheese and pepperoni but they have others that stand out like their vegan chorizo or their spicy red sauce, this one is recommended.Customizing your pizza is easy since all of the toppings are labeled and the folks behind the counter are always willing to add more of your preferred topping or sauce if requested.

For drinks they offer beer on tap or bottled, aguas frescas and other drinks in bottles on top of fountain drinks.

Salads are also offered, but I have never ordered one.

Pretty good choice if you wanna sit down to eat or on the go.< /Text>

< review>
My girlfriend's Macbook Air started randomly shutting down for no foreseeable reason, so we did a google search for macbook repair places, and BDJ came up. She brought the laptop in and met with Jose (without me - I had to work). He was a little rough around the edges from the get go, but seemed to know what he was doing. He opened her laptop and told her to feel the processor, trying to support his diagnosis of overheating being the problem. This was the first sign of trouble, as anyone who works on computers knows that feeling a processor will not tell you if it's overheating as processors often get above 150 degrees while staying within normal range of operation. He told her that the fix was to replace the logic board and that it this would cost ~$350.  She paid, and he told her he had to order the logic board and that she should bring the laptop back after he called us to let us know it had arrived.

She came home and we looked at her laptop. I did some of the diagnostic stuff they do at the Apple store and it quickly became apparent that this was a battery/charger issue and most likely had nothing to do with the logic board. I called and spoke to Jose to try explain my thoughts and perhaps get a refund for the $350 she had already paid since a battery replacement wouldn't be this much. He immediately started becoming VERY agitated and trying to rush me off the phone, saying he had other customers he had to help. He kept insisting that the logic board was the issue. The longer I kept him on the phone trying to explain the logic behind my theory, the more and more rude he became, explaining that "I told your girl to feel the processor. I told her! Have her explain to you! I don't have time. I have other customers here to take care of!" I asked him if he would refund the money if he did indeed replace the logic board, and it turned out that wasn't the issue, and he promised he would provide the refund.

Flash forward 2-weeks, I called again to see if the logic board had come in. It took him 3 tries to find the correct customer account after I gave him the invoice number he provided when we paid. He explained that the logic board had arrived and that we could bring the laptop in. We dropped it off the next day, and he called 3 days later to say the work was done.

Upon bringing the Macbook home, within the first hour or so, it began randomly shutting down just like before. I ordered a new genuine Apple magsafe charger, and low-and-behold, it stopped shutting down and everything was fine once again. This of course proved my theory that it was a power issue and not the logic board. I called Jose back and tried to explain this. He almost immediately became irate and started making all sorts of strange claims. One, he said that he was not able to test the laptop because my girlfriend "never gave him her password". He never once asked for said password, as we would have obliged if it meant he would be able to fix the issue. He then told me to bring the laptop back in, but by then, I was so appalled by the way he had spoken to me that I told him I did not want to do business with him anymore and asked that he please provide the refund he originally promised. He declined and repeated that I needed to bring the computer back in. I spent about 10 minutes on the phone with him, trying to reason with him, politely asking for the refund, explaining how what he had done did not fix the issue and how a simple charger replacement did the trick. He would not hear it and began using the "I have other customers I have to take care of" line as before. Finally, he one last time said "You want help, bring the computer back in!" and hung up the phone.

We didn't bring it back to him. As a paying customer, I've never been spoken to like Jose spoke to me on the phone, and I would highly recommend you stay away from this place. There are plenty of other Apple repair shops in the valley. You may pay a bit more elsewhere, but at least you'll avoid getting yelled at and lied to.</review>

<Review>When I was growing up, in the 1960s, if the family television began to act up my father would remove the tubes, take them down to the drugstore, diagnose the bad tube and replace it.  Component level repair was the norm.  Sometime during the 70's or 80's  we as a nation seemed to collectively forget  how to repair our products at the component level and, with computers in particular, when a component fails (e.g. a surface mounted IC), we toss out the entire board and replace it --- throwing away hundreds of working components.  This is wasteful, costly, lazy and stupid.

Jose at BDJ is a talented technician who diagnoses which component on a board has failed and uses special manufacturing tools (surface mount IC) to replace just the component.  A repair to my system board that would have cost $750 anywhere else, cost just $200 here.  It was completed in two work days with a smile and not a promise broken.

Go to BDJ, not just to save a few hundred bucks (you will), but to help save the environment from excessive waste and help save the country from stupidity.  Thanks Jose!<//Review><response>None<//response><time>1445992967064</time><Rate>5<//Rate><pics>None< /pics><user_id>108091348874460777585< /user_id><gmap_id>0x80c2b863b26ad8e5:0x61c0d5bf3a12dc91<//gmap_id></record>
